### [1] [Superpixel Attack: Enhancing Black-box Adversarial Attack with Image-driven Division Areas](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02062)
*Issa Oe,Keiichiro Yamamura,Hiroki Ishikura,Ryo Hamahira,Katsuki Fujisawa*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 将超像素与新搜索方法结合用于黑盒对抗攻击，在稳健模型上平均提升2.10%成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有黑盒攻击在每次迭代仅修改矩形区域，局限于形状与语义一致性，超像素能更好地捕捉图像局部结构，从而提高攻击效率。

Method: 基于重复提取图像特定区域并修改扰动的思想，使用超像素分割得到颜色方差与紧凑性平衡的区域，结合新搜索策略(versatile search)迭代寻找有效扰动。

Result: 在多种稳健模型上，Superpixel Attack平均比现有方法提高2.10%的攻击成功率，代码已开源。

Conclusion: 提出Superpixel Attack，使用超像素替代矩形区域并引入versatile search，显著提升黑盒攻击成功率。

Abstract: Deep learning models are used in safety-critical tasks such as automated driving and face recognition. However, small perturbations in the model input can significantly change the predictions. Adversarial attacks are used to identify small perturbations that can lead to misclassifications. More powerful black-box adversarial attacks are required to develop more effective defenses. A promising approach to black-box adversarial attacks is to repeat the process of extracting a specific image area and changing the perturbations added to it. Existing attacks adopt simple rectangles as the areas where perturbations are changed in a single iteration. We propose applying superpixels instead, which achieve a good balance between color variance and compactness. We also propose a new search method, versatile search, and a novel attack method, Superpixel Attack, which applies superpixels and performs versatile search. Superpixel Attack improves attack success rates by an average of 2.10% compared with existing attacks. Most models used in this study are robust against adversarial attacks, and this improvement is significant for black-box adversarial attacks. The code is avilable at https://github.com/oe1307/SuperpixelAttack.git.

</details>


### [2] [Large Language Model based Smart Contract Auditing with LLMBugScanner](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02069)
*Yining Yuan,Yifei Wang,Yichang Xu,Zachary Yahn,Sihao Hu,Ling Liu*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: LLMBugScanner fine-tunes multiple LLMs on complementary datasets using parameter-efficient tuning, then ensembles them with consensus-based conflict resolution for more reliable smart contract vulnerability detection, improving accuracy and generalization.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Single LLMs vary across vulnerability types and structures; need robustness and generalization in smart contract auditing.

Method: Fine-tuning + Ensemble

Result: Ensemble of fine-tuned LLMs with domain adaptation and consensus conflict resolution yields consistent accuracy improvements and better generalization.

Conclusion: LLMBugScanner is a cost-effective, extensible framework that leverages domain adaptation and ensemble reasoning to address LLM inconsistencies, achieving stronger auditing performance than individual models.

Abstract: This paper presents LLMBugScanner, a large language model (LLM) based framework for smart contract vulnerability detection using fine-tuning and ensemble learning. Smart contract auditing presents several challenges for LLMs: different pretrained models exhibit varying reasoning abilities, and no single model performs consistently well across all vulnerability types or contract structures. These limitations persist even after fine-tuning individual LLMs.
  To address these challenges, LLMBugScanner combines domain knowledge adaptation with ensemble reasoning to improve robustness and generalization. Through domain knowledge adaptation, we fine-tune LLMs on complementary datasets to capture both general code semantics and instruction-guided vulnerability reasoning, using parameter-efficient tuning to reduce computational cost. Through ensemble reasoning, we leverage the complementary strengths of multiple LLMs and apply a consensus-based conflict resolution strategy to produce more reliable vulnerability assessments.
  We conduct extensive experiments across multiple popular LLMs and compare LLMBugScanner with both pretrained and fine-tuned individual models. Results show that LLMBugScanner achieves consistent accuracy improvements and stronger generalization, demonstrating that it provides a principled, cost-effective, and extensible framework for smart contract auditing.

</details>


### [3] [Deterministic Random Bit Generators Based on Ascon for Embedded Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02082)
*Abel C. H. Chen*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 利用Ascon设计三种轻量级DRBG并在树莓派上验证，性能和内存均优于现有实现，适合资源受限的嵌入式应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 嵌入式系统受限于内存和计算资源，传统DRBG在这些平台上可能不够高效。NIST在2025年采纳Ascon为轻量级密码标准，激励使用Ascon构建适合嵌入式的高效安全DRBG。

Method: 在现有DRBG标准基础上，用Ascon替换或重构核心函数，设计三种构造：Ascon-Driven Hash-Based（以Ascon散列替代哈希函数）、Ascon-Driven HMAC（用Ascon构建HMAC）和Ascon-Driven CTR（以Ascon作为块函数的计数器模式）。在树莓派平台上实现并测量运行时间与内存占用，与现有实现比较。

Result: 实验显示三种Ascon驱动的DRBG在计算效率更高、内存使用更低，满足嵌入式系统需求；具体指标（如吞吐率、延迟、RAM占用）在论文中给出并显著优于对照实现。

Conclusion: 提出并评估基于Ascon的三种DRBG构造（Hash-Based、HMAC、CTR），在树莓派上实现，结果显示在性能和内存占用方面优于现有实现，适用于嵌入式系统。

Abstract: As the Deterministic Random Bit Generator (DRBG) serves as a fundamental component in random number generation and cryptographic applications, its performance and security are particularly critical in resource-constrained embedded systems, where memory capacity and computational efficiency are limited. Establishing a high-performance and secure DRBG is therefore an important issue for embedded system design. Furthermore, the National Institute of Standards and Technology (NIST) established the Ascon lightweight cryptographic standard in August 2025, which is suitable for use in resource-limited embedded environments. Therefore, this study revises the DRBG standard and proposes three Ascon-driven constructions: the Ascon-Driven Hash-Based DRBG, the Ascon-Driven keyed-Hash Message Authentication Code (HMAC) DRBG, and the Ascon-Driven Counter-mode (CTR) DRBG. In the experiments, these methods are implemented on a Raspberry Pi platform. The experimental results demonstrate that the proposed approaches achieve higher computational efficiency and lower memory usage compared with existing DRBG implementations, making them suitable for deployment in embedded systems.

</details>


### [4] [A survey about Hidden Subgroup Problem from a mathematical and cryptographic perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02087)
*Simone Dutto,Pietro Mercuri,Nadir Murru,Lorenzo Romano*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 综述 HSP：阿贝尔群已被量子高效解决（Kitaev 等），非阿贝尔群仍困难，研究集中在二面体群、对称群与半直积，主要技术为傅里叶采样与黑盒方法，强调对密码学安全性的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解 HSP 的算法学进展有助于评估基于不同数学结构的公钥密码方案的量子安全性，尤其需要把密码学问题表述为 HSP 实例以便利用量子算法的潜在威胁。

Method: 通过回顾阿贝尔 HSP 的量子算法（Kitaev 算法）与经典问题的对应，并总结非阿贝尔情形中的主要攻关技术（傅里叶采样和黑盒方法），对相关群结构和数学工具进行说明与比较分析。

Result: 整理并归纳了阿贝尔情形的高效量子解法与将经典困难问题表述为阿贝尔 HSP 的方法，详细讨论了非阿贝尔 HSP 在特定群上的复杂性、已知技术的局限性和与密码学相关的问题映射。

Conclusion: 该论文综述了隐藏子群问题（HSP）在密码学中的重要性，指出在阿贝尔群情形下有高效量子算法（Kitaev 等），而在非阿贝尔群情形下仍无通用高效解，强调了若干重要群（如二面体群、对称群和半直积构造）及其与实际密码学问题（最短向量问题、图同构、码等价）之间的联系。

Abstract: We provide a survey on the Hidden Subgroup Problem (HSP), which plays an important role in studying the security of public-key cryptosystems. We first review the abelian case, where Kitaev's algorithm yields an efficient quantum solution to the HSP, recalling how classical problems (such as order finding, integer factorization, and discrete logarithm) can be formulated as abelian HSP instances. We then examine the current state of the art for non-abelian HSP, where no general efficient quantum solution is known, focusing on some relevant groups including dihedral group (connected to the shortest vector problem), symmetric groups (connected to the graph isomorphism problem), and semidirect product constructions (connected, in a special case, to the code equivalence problem). We also describe the main techniques for addressing the HSP in non-abelian cases, namely Fourier sampling and the black-box approach. Throughout the paper, we highlight the mathematical notions required and exploited in this context, providing a cryptography-oriented perspective.

</details>


### [5] [Factor(T,U): Factored Cognition Strengthens Monitoring of Untrusted AI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02157)
*Aaron Sandoval,Cody Rushing*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 在APPS代码生成任务中，使用事实化认知分解任务并由可信模型监控子任务，能显著提升检测不安全代码的成功率（41%→63%），主要因为监控器在简化上下文中更有效，但并不能阻止强大LLM写后门，且在APPS上实际效用有限，需在更复杂场景中进一步验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决现有依赖弱监控器检测不安全行为的方法在复杂任务上失效的问题。通过将复杂任务拆成多个子任务，使监控器在简化、局部的上下文中运行，从而提高其识别恶意或不安全行为的能力，同时可能通过限制环境上下文暴露来减少攻击面与脆弱性利用。

Method: 提出一种基于事实化认知的控制协议：由可信模型负责任务分解并组装答案，未受信任模型独立解决子任务；在APPS代码生成任务中实现该协议，并进行对抗测试（red team）——使用攻击性GPT-4.1 Nano尝试在代码中植入后门，评估带/不带事实化认知的监控协议对检测与防护的效果。

Result: 关键结果包括：(i) 在APPS基准与红队攻击下，加入事实化认知的监控协议将安全检测率从41%提升到63%；(ii) 安全性提升的主要原因是监控器在子任务层面的表现改善；(iii) 事实化认知并未阻止强大模型编写后门，APPS任务中该协议对实际效用有限。研究指出方法在更复杂任务上仍有潜力。

Conclusion: 该论文提出将事实化认知（factored cognition）用于AI控制协议，通过可信模型分解任务、非可信模型分别解决子任务并重组结果，以期改善对不受信任AI的监控与防护。实验证明在APPS编码环境中，加入事实化认知能将检测到不安全行为的成功率从41%提升到63%，其提升因监控器在更简化上下文中的表现改善；但这种方法并未增加强大LLM（如GPT-4.1 Nano）编写后门的难度，且在APPS任务上的实际效用较低。总体结论是方法在更复杂任务上具有潜力，但当前验证有限，仍需进一步研究。

Abstract: The field of AI Control seeks to develop robust control protocols, deployment safeguards for untrusted AI which may be intentionally subversive. However, existing protocols that rely on weaker monitors to detect unsafe behavior often fail on complex tasks beyond the monitor's comprehension. We develop control protocols based on factored cognition, in which a trusted model decomposes a task, an untrusted model solves each resultant child task in isolation, and the results are reassembled into a full solution. These protocols may improve safety by several means, such as by simplifying the context for monitors, or by obscuring vulnerabilities in the environment. We implement our protocols in the APPS coding setting and red team them against backdoor attempts from an adversarial GPT-4.1 Nano. We find that: (i) Adding factored cognition to a trusted monitoring protocol can boost safety from 41% to 63%; (ii) Safety improves because monitor performance improves; (iii) Factored cognition makes it no harder for capable LLMs to write backdoors in APPS. While our protocols show low usefulness in APPS, they hold promise for more complex tasks.

</details>


### [6] [PhishSnap: Image-Based Phishing Detection Using Perceptual Hashing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02243)
*Md Abdul Ahad Minhaz,Zannatul Zahan Meem,Md. Shohrab Hossain*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: PhishSnap作为本地感知哈希浏览器扩展，能在保护隐私的前提下通过视觉相似性检测钓鱼页面，性能中等（准确率约0.79），但受数据偏差和视觉对抗的限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有URL和HTML检测易被混淆和视觉欺骗绕过，因此提出基于页面视觉相似性的本地化检测以增强隐私与对抗可视伪装的能力。

Method: 在浏览器扩展内截取网页截图，计算感知哈希（pHash），与合法站点模板哈希比对以检测视觉相似的钓鱼页面，全部推理在本地完成。

Result: 使用2024年收集的10000个URL数据集进行训练/验证/测试，报告准确率0.79、精确率0.76、召回率0.78。部分钓鱼页面因下线导致样本多样性受限。

Conclusion: PhishSnap通过基于视觉哈希的本地化检测在保护隐私的同时能有效识别一定比例的仿冒页面，但性能受数据集偏差与视觉相似性局限影响，尚不足以完全替代其他检测手段。

Abstract: Phishing remains one of the most prevalent online threats, exploiting human trust to harvest sensitive credentials. Existing URL- and HTML-based detection systems struggle against obfuscation and visual deception. This paper presents \textbf{PhishSnap}, a privacy-preserving, on-device phishing detection system leveraging perceptual hashing (pHash). Implemented as a browser extension, PhishSnap captures webpage screenshots, computes visual hashes, and compares them against legitimate templates to identify visually similar phishing attempts. A \textbf{2024 dataset of 10,000 URLs} (70\%/20\%/10\% train/validation/test) was collected from PhishTank and Netcraft. Due to security takedowns, a subset of phishing pages was unavailable, reducing dataset diversity. The system achieved \textbf{0.79 accuracy}, \textbf{0.76 precision}, and \textbf{0.78 recall}, showing that visual similarity remains a viable anti-phishing measure. The entire inference process occurs locally, ensuring user privacy and minimal latency.

</details>


### [7] [CVE Breadcrumbs: Tracking Vulnerabilities Through Versioned Apache Libraries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02259)
*Derek Garcia,Briana Lee,Ibrahim Matar,David Rickards,Andrew Zilnicki*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 对Apache生态的1,285个CVE和157个CWE的历史分析显示：少数CWE反复导致高影响漏洞，漏洞从引入到披露与修复存在较长延迟，需加强静态检测、依赖治理与快速补丁策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Apache生态支撑大量关键基础设施组件，历史上发生过高影响事件（如Log4Shell），提示需要系统性研究漏洞为何反复出现、修复迟缓及披露过程中的盲点，以改善开发和运维实践。

Method: 通过收集并整理来自Apache项目的24,285个库、1,285个CVE和157个CWE，构建时间线与元数据，统计分析漏洞复现频率、披露与修复时长，并按CWE分类进行趋势分析。

Result: 发现若干高频反复的CWE（如不安全的输入处理、认证/授权错误和配置不当），CVEs在代码库中存在时间显著长于修复后公开的窗口，披露前的引入延迟和披露后修复延迟均存在显著差异；并基于这些发现提出具体的开发者监测与修复建议。

Conclusion: 本研究揭示了Apache生态中若干长期反复出现的安全弱点（主要CWE类型）、漏洞从引入到披露及修复的典型时间延迟，并指出现有漏洞管理的不足与改进方向。

Abstract: The Apache Software Foundation (ASF) ecosystem underpins a vast portion of modern software infrastructure, powering widely used components such as Log4j, Tomcat, and Struts. However, the ubiquity of these libraries has made them prime targets for high-impact security vulnerabilities, as illustrated by incidents like Log4Shell. Despite their widespread adoption, Apache projects are not immune to recurring and severe security weaknesses. We conduct a historical analysis of the Apache ecosystem to follow the "breadcrumb trail of vulnerabilities" by compiling a comprehensive dataset of Common Vulnerabilities and Exposures (CVEs) and Common Weakness Enumerations (CWEs). We examine trends in exploit recurrence, disclosure timelines, and remediation practices. Our analysis is guided by four key research questions: (1) What are the most persistent and repeated CWEs in Apache libraries? (2) How long do CVEs persist before being addressed? (3) What is the delay between CVE introduction and official disclosure? and (4) How long after disclosure are CVEs remediated? We present a detailed timeline of vulnerability lifecycle stages across Apache libraries and offer insights to improve secure coding practices, vulnerability monitoring, and remediation strategies. Our contributions include a curated dataset covering 24,285 Apache libraries, 1,285 CVEs, and 157 CWEs, along with empirical findings and developer-focused recommendations.

</details>


### [8] [Property-Guided Cyber-Physical Reduction and Surrogation for Safety Analysis in Robotic Vehicles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02270)
*Nazmus Shakib Sayom,Luis Garcia*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 按性质缩减控制器并在轻量替代体上做逻辑感知的测试，可高效、低成本地发现无人机等网络物理系统的安全语义缺陷。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 完整系统仿真成本高且包含大量与安全性质无关的复杂性，阻碍了基于测试的语义验证；通过缩减到与性质相关的子系统可以显著提升测试效率并保持发现真实缺陷的能力。

Method: 基于给定安全性质对系统进行分析，提取仅与该性质相关的控制和物理动态模块，构建替代模型（surrogate）并在其上运行基于轨迹分析和时序逻辑的模糊测试（property-guided fuzzer）与oracle判定，以进行可扩展的伪证（falsification）。

Result: 在含已知安全缺陷的无人机控制系统上验证：替代模型在远低于原始仿真成本下复制了导致失效的条件，结合性质引导的模糊测试能高效触发语义违规，证明方法在可扩展语义验证中的可行性。

Conclusion: 该方法通过有针对性地缩减控制逻辑与动力学模型，构造保留与性质相关行为的轻量替代体，从而在保持相关性前提下大幅降低仿真成本，能够有效发现机器人车辆系统的语义安全缺陷。

Abstract: We propose a methodology for falsifying safety properties in robotic vehicle systems through property-guided reduction and surrogate execution. By isolating only the control logic and physical dynamics relevant to a given specification, we construct lightweight surrogate models that preserve property-relevant behaviors while eliminating unrelated system complexity. This enables scalable falsification via trace analysis and temporal logic oracles.
  We demonstrate the approach on a drone control system containing a known safety flaw. The surrogate replicates failure conditions at a fraction of the simulation cost, and a property-guided fuzzer efficiently discovers semantic violations. Our results suggest that controller reduction, when coupled with logic-aware test generation, provides a practical and scalable path toward semantic verification of cyber-physical systems.

</details>


### [9] [HOT Protocol](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02287)
*Peter Volnov,Georgii Kuksa,Andrey Zhevlakov*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: HOT uses TEE-backed MPC to let smart contracts own private keys, managed by an MPC Network and integrated with NEAR for state; works across Stellar, TON, Solana, and EVM chains.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Provide secure on-chain key management allowing smart contracts to own keys while reducing participant economic requirements and improving security via TEE-enabled MPC.

Method: MPC Network manages signing keys with nodes running inside TEEs; integration with NEAR Protocol for decentralized state; compatibility layers for Stellar, TON, Solana, and EVM chains.

Result: Stronger security guarantees for key management, reduced economic barriers for participants, and broad compatibility across multiple blockchain ecosystems.

Conclusion: HOT Protocol enables smart contracts to securely hold/manage private keys by combining MPC and TEE, integrated with NEAR for state layer and cross-chain compatibility.

Abstract: HOT Protocol provides the infrastructure that allows smart contracts to securely own and manage private keys. The Multi-Party Computation (MPC) Network manages signing keys. By running an MPC node inside a Trusted Execution Environment (TEE), the protocol achieves stronger security guarantees while lowering economic requirements for participants. The NEAR Protocol provides a decentralized and efficient state layer. Key management can be integrated with any smart contract across Stellar, TON, Solana, and EVM-compatible networks.

</details>


### [10] [Quantum Vanguard: Server Optimized Privacy Fortified Federated Intelligence for Future Vehicles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02301)
*Dev Gurung,Shiva Raj Pokhrel*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 提出vQFL：将量子联邦学习、差分隐私与QKD结合，并用服务器端微调(ft-VQFL)提升性能。实验证明此框架在自动驾驶车联网中能提供量子抗性隐私与通信安全，同时保持模型效能与低开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 应对量子计算威胁以及传统隐私泄露问题，保障自动驾驶车辆在大规模数据生成（20-40TB/天/车）与分布式学习场景中的模型隐私与通信安全，同时保持模型效能与低通信成本。

Method: 设计vQFL架构：客户端（车辆）使用变分量子电路等量子模型训练本地模型，结合差分隐私机制对梯度或参数进行噪声注入；通过QKD建立安全通信信道并进行密钥管理；服务器端采用ft-VQFL微调聚合模型以提升鲁棒性。实现多种量子模型（VQC、QCNN、SamplerQNN），并在真实行业数据集上进行通信与隐私性能评估和开销测试。

Result: 在KITTI、Waymo、nuScenes上的实验表明：vQFL在模型精度上与标准QFL相当；使用差分隐私与QKD后隐私保障显著增强；通信安全性对抗量子攻击能力提升；不同量子模型引入的额外计算与通信开销较低；ft-VQFL进一步提高了聚合模型的鲁棒性和收敛速度。

Conclusion: vQFL提出了将量子联邦学习与差分隐私和量子密钥分发相结合的框架，可在自动驾驶车联网中提升隐私与通信安全，并通过服务器端微调(ft-VQFL)增强性能和鲁棒性。实验在KITTI、Waymo、nuScenes上显示在保证隐私与安全的同时，准确率与标准QFL相当，且不同量子模型带来性能开销很小。框架模块化，便于与现有车联网集成，为后量子时代自动驾驶系统提供基础。

Abstract: This work presents vQFL (vehicular Quantum Federated Learning), a new framework that leverages quantum machine learning techniques to tackle key privacy and security issues in autonomous vehicular networks. Furthermore, we propose a server-side adapted fine-tuning method, ft-VQFL,to achieve enhanced and more resilient performance. By integrating quantum federated learning with differential privacy and quantum key distribution (QKD), our quantum vanguard approach creates a multi-layered defense against both classical and quantum threats while preserving model utility. Extensive experimentation with industry-standard datasets (KITTI, Waymo, and nuScenes) demonstrates that vQFL maintains accuracy comparable to standard QFL while significantly improving privacy guaranties and communication security. Our implementation using various quantum models (VQC, QCNN, and SamplerQNN) reveals minimal performance overhead despite the added security measures. This work establishes a crucial foundation for quantum-resistant autonomous vehicle systems that can operate securely in the post-quantum era while efficiently processing the massive data volumes (20-40TB/day per vehicle) generated by modern autonomous fleets. The modular design of the framework allows for seamless integration with existing vehicular networks, positioning vQFL as an essential component for future intelligent transportation infrastructure.

</details>


### [11] [COGNITION: From Evaluation to Defense against Multimodal LLM CAPTCHA Solvers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02318)
*Junyu Wang,Changjia Zhu,Yuanbo Zhou,Lingyao Li,Xu He,Junjie Xiong*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: Study shows MLLMs can break many visual CAPTCHAs cheaply and quickly, but tasks requiring fine spatial reasoning or consistency remain more robust; offers practical defense recommendations.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Determine whether modern MLLMs can automate solving visual CAPTCHAs and identify which CAPTCHA designs remain robust, providing guidance for platform operators.

Method: Empirical evaluation of 7 commercial/open-source MLLMs across 18 real-world CAPTCHA types, measuring single-shot accuracy, retry-limited success, latency, cost; experiments on prompt engineering and few-shot examples; analysis of model reasoning traces.

Result: MLLMs achieve high success on recognition-oriented/low-interaction CAPTCHAs with human-like cost/latency; they fail more on tasks needing precise localization, multi-step spatial reasoning, or cross-frame consistency. Prompting/few-shot help but don't fully bridge gaps. Defense guidelines proposed.

Conclusion: MLLMs significantly weaken many visual CAPTCHA types, reliably solving recognition-oriented and low-interaction tasks at near-human cost/latency, while struggles remain for fine-grained localization, multi-step spatial reasoning, and cross-frame consistency; defenses should prioritize those harder properties and combine multiple modalities.

Abstract: This paper studies how multimodal large language models (MLLMs) undermine the security guarantees of visual CAPTCHA. We identify the attack surface where an adversary can cheaply automate CAPTCHA solving using off-the-shelf models. We evaluate 7 leading commercial and open-source MLLMs across 18 real-world CAPTCHA task types, measuring single-shot accuracy, success under limited retries, end-to-end latency, and per-solve cost. We further analyze the impact of task-specific prompt engineering and few-shot demonstrations on solver effectiveness. We reveal that MLLMs can reliably solve recognition-oriented and low-interaction CAPTCHA tasks at human-like cost and latency, whereas tasks requiring fine-grained localization, multi-step spatial reasoning, or cross-frame consistency remain significantly harder for current models. By examining the reasoning traces of such MLLMs, we investigate the underlying mechanisms of why models succeed/fail on specific CAPTCHA puzzles and use these insights to derive defense-oriented guidelines for selecting and strengthening CAPTCHA tasks. We conclude by discussing implications for platform operators deploying CAPTCHA as part of their abuse-mitigation pipeline.Code Availability (https://anonymous.4open.science/r/Captcha-465E/).

### [12] [LeechHijack: Covert Computational Resource Exploitation in Intelligent Agent Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02321)
*Yuanhe Zhang,Weiliu Wang,Zhenhong Zhou,Kun Wang,Jie Zhang,Li Sun,Yang Liu,Sen Su*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 论文发现并实现了一种在MCP生态下利用合法权限滥用计算资源的攻击（LeechHijack），并在多种LLM上验证其高成功率，建议引入计算证明和资源溯源机制以防护。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: MCP的开放性与可组合性虽促进生态繁荣，但默认信任第三方工具带来安全隐患；研究动机是发现并形式化这种在显式权限范围内发生的恶意行为。

Method: 通过构造两阶段攻击（植入含后门的工具 + 利用触发器建立命令与控制通道），在四个主流LLM家族上实现并评估LeechHijack，测量成功率和资源开销。

Result: 在四个主流LLM家族上的实验表明平均攻击成功率为77.25%，资源开销为18.62%，证明攻击可行且有效。

Conclusion: 该论文揭示了MCP生态中“隐式毒性”攻击的新风险，提出并实现了LeechHijack攻击，说明第三方工具在权限范围内也能滥用计算资源，呼吁引入计算来源和资源证明机制。

Abstract: Large Language Model (LLM)-based agents have demonstrated remarkable capabilities in reasoning, planning, and tool usage. The recently proposed Model Context Protocol (MCP) has emerged as a unifying framework for integrating external tools into agent systems, enabling a thriving open ecosystem of community-built functionalities. However, the openness and composability that make MCP appealing also introduce a critical yet overlooked security assumption -- implicit trust in third-party tool providers. In this work, we identify and formalize a new class of attacks that exploit this trust boundary without violating explicit permissions. We term this new attack vector implicit toxicity, where malicious behaviors occur entirely within the allowed privilege scope. We propose LeechHijack, a Latent Embedded Exploit for Computation Hijacking, in which an adversarial MCP tool covertly expropriates the agent's computational resources for unauthorized workloads. LeechHijack operates through a two-stage mechanism: an implantation stage that embeds a benign-looking backdoor in a tool, and an exploitation stage where the backdoor activates upon predefined triggers to establish a command-and-control channel. Through this channel, the attacker injects additional tasks that the agent executes as if they were part of its normal workflow, effectively parasitizing the user's compute budget. We implement LeechHijack across four major LLM families. Experiments show that LeechHijack achieves an average success rate of 77.25%, with a resource overhead of 18.62% compared to the baseline. This study highlights the urgent need for computational provenance and resource attestation mechanisms to safeguard the emerging MCP ecosystem.

*Xiaoqi Li,Zongwei Li,Wenkai Li,Zeng Zhang,Lei Xie*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有工具在检测智能合约原子性违规时精度不足，需要一种能融合结构与语义信息的自动化高精度检测方法。

Method: 构建基于图卷积网络的检测框架，采用协同学习机制同时从CFG提取结构拓扑特征和从操作码序列提取深层语义特征，使用自适应加权融合动态调整模态权重，最终在图级别进行原子性违规分类。

Abstract: Smart contracts are a core component of blockchain technology and are widely deployed across various scenarios. However, atomicity violations have become a potential security risk. Existing analysis tools often lack the precision required to detect these issues effectively. To address this challenge, we introduce AtomGraph, an automated framework designed for detecting atomicity violations. This framework leverages Graph Convolutional Networks (GCN) to identify atomicity violations through multimodal feature learning and fusion. Specifically, driven by a collaborative learning mechanism, the model simultaneously learns from two heterogeneous modalities: extracting structural topological features from the contract's Control Flow Graph (CFG) and uncovering deep semantics from its opcode sequence. We designed an adaptive weighted fusion mechanism to dynamically adjust the weights of features from each modality to achieve optimal feature fusion. Finally, GCN detects graph-level atomicity violation on the contract. Comprehensive experimental evaluations demonstrate that AtomGraph achieves 96.88% accuracy and 96.97% F1 score, outperforming existing tools. Furthermore, compared to the concatenation fusion model, AtomGraph improves the F1 score by 6.4%, proving its potential in smart contract security detection.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Cybersecurity of space infrastructures is an emerging topic, despite space-related cybersecurity incidents occurring as early as 1977 (i.e., hijacking of a satellite transmission signal). There is no single dataset that documents cyber attacks against space infrastructures that have occurred in the past; instead, these incidents are often scattered in media reports while missing many details, which we dub the missing-data problem. Nevertheless, even ``low-quality'' datasets containing such reports would be extremely valuable because of the dearth of space cybersecurity data and the sensitivity of space infrastructures which are often restricted from disclosure by governments. This prompts a research question: How can we characterize real-world cyber attacks against space infrastructures? In this paper, we address the problem by proposing a framework, including metrics, while also addressing the missing-data problem by leveraging methodologies such as the Space Attack Research and Tactic Analysis (SPARTA) and the Adversarial Tactics, Techniques, and Common Knowledge (ATT&CK) to ``extrapolate'' the missing data in a principled fashion. We show how the extrapolated data can be used to reconstruct ``hypothetical but plausible'' space cyber kill chains and space cyber attack campaigns that have occurred in practice. To show the usefulness of the framework, we extract data for 108 cyber attacks against space infrastructures and show how to extrapolate this ``low-quality'' dataset containing missing information to derive 6,206 attack technique-level space cyber kill chains. Our findings include: cyber attacks against space infrastructures are getting increasingly sophisticated; successful protection of the link segment between the space and user segments could have thwarted nearly half of the 108 attacks. We will make our dataset available.

However, due to the refined division of labor, crowdsourcing laundering transactions exhibit diverse patterns and a polycentric structure, posing significant challenges for detection. In this paper, we introduce transaction group as auxiliary information, and propose the Multi-Task Collaborative Crowdsourcing Laundering Detection (MCCLD) framework. MCCLD employs an end-to-end graph neural network to realize collaboration between laundering transaction detection and transaction group detection tasks, enhancing detection performance on diverse patterns within crowdsourcing laundering group. These two tasks are jointly optimized through a shared classifier, with a shared feature encoder that fuses multi-level feature embeddings to provide rich transaction semantics and potential group information. Extensive experiments on both crowdsourcing and general laundering demonstrate MCCLD's effectiveness and generalization. To the best of our knowledge, this is the first work on crowdsourcing laundering detection.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前LLM在深度推理和复杂数学分析（如加密学）能力的评估与训练上缺乏合适数据集，阻碍了其在密码学研究与开发中的应用。需要一个专门的数据集来全面测试并提升模型在加密学上的能力。

Method: 构建包含200万+问答对的CryptoQA数据集，来源为经挑选的学术资料，并附带上下文元数据；对15个最先进的大型语言模型进行多维基准测试（事实准确率、数学推理、一致性、引用、逆向推理、对抗样本鲁棒性）；提供专家定性评审并建立金标准基线；演示使用CryptoQA进行微调可提升模型在加密学任务上的表现。

Result: 基准测试显示多模型在涉及形式化推理与精确数学知识的问题上表现欠佳；专家评审 corroborates quantitative findings；通过在CryptoQA上微调，模型在加密学任务上的表现得到改善，但仍存在显著缺陷，表明需开发专门的加密学LLM助理。

Conclusion: LLMs目前在加密学任务上表现明显不足，尤其是需要形式化推理和精确数学知识的场景；CryptoQA作为首个大规模加密学QA数据集，可用于评估与微调，从而提升模型在加密领域的能力。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) excel at many general-purpose natural language processing tasks. However, their ability to perform deep reasoning and mathematical analysis, particularly for complex tasks as required in cryptography, remains poorly understood, largely due to the lack of suitable data for evaluation and training. To address this gap, we present CryptoQA, the first large-scale question-answering (QA) dataset specifically designed for cryptography. CryptoQA contains over two million QA pairs drawn from curated academic sources, along with contextual metadata that can be used to test the cryptographic capabilities of LLMs and to train new LLMs on cryptographic tasks. We benchmark 15 state-of-the-art LLMs on CryptoQA, evaluating their factual accuracy, mathematical reasoning, consistency, referencing, backward reasoning, and robustness to adversarial samples. In addition to quantitative metrics, we provide expert reviews that qualitatively assess model outputs and establish a gold-standard baseline. Our results reveal significant performance deficits of LLMs, particularly on tasks that require formal reasoning and precise mathematical knowledge. This shows the urgent need for LLM assistants tailored to cryptography research and development. We demonstrate that, by using CryptoQA, LLMs can be fine-tuned to exhibit better performance on cryptographic tasks.

</details>


### [21] [Cybersecurity AI: The World's Top AI Agent for Security Capture-the-Flag (CTF)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02654)
*Víctor Mayoral-Vilches,Luis Javier Navarrete-Lozano,Francesco Balassone,María Sanz-Gómez,Cristóbal R. J. Veas Chavez,Maite del Mundo de Torres,Vanesa Turiel*

Conclusion: 本文结论认为：在2025年，专用的AI代理（CAI）已系统性地主宰Jeopardy式CTF竞赛，使该类比赛对评估顶尖安全人才的效力受到严重质疑，安全社区应转向更能考察适应性推理与抗毁性（如攻防赛）的竞赛形式。

Abstract: Are Capture-the-Flag competitions obsolete? In 2025, Cybersecurity AI (CAI) systematically conquered some of the world's most prestigious hacking competitions, achieving Rank #1 at multiple events and consistently outperforming thousands of human teams. Across five major circuits-HTB's AI vs Humans, Cyber Apocalypse (8,129 teams), Dragos OT CTF, UWSP Pointer Overflow, and the Neurogrid CTF showdown-CAI demonstrated that Jeopardy-style CTFs have become a solved game for well-engineered AI agents. At Neurogrid, CAI captured 41/45 flags to claim the $50,000 top prize; at Dragos OT, it sprinted 37% faster to 10K points than elite human teams; even when deliberately paused mid-competition, it maintained top-tier rankings. Critically, CAI achieved this dominance through our specialized alias1 model architecture, which delivers enterprise-scale AI security operations at unprecedented cost efficiency and with augmented autonomy-reducing 1B token inference costs from $5,940 to just $119, making continuous security agent operation financially viable for the first time. These results force an uncomfortable reckoning: if autonomous agents now dominate competitions designed to identify top security talent at negligible cost, what are CTFs actually measuring? This paper presents comprehensive evidence of AI capability across the 2025 CTF circuit and argues that the security community must urgently transition from Jeopardy-style contests to Attack & Defense formats that genuinely test adaptive reasoning and resilience-capabilities that remain uniquely human, for now.

</details>


### [22] [Decryption thorough polynomial ambiguity: noise-enhanced high-memory convolutional codes for post-quantum cryptography](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02822)
*Meir Ariel*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 论文提出用高记忆卷积码的有向图解码并在解码时注入多项式噪声来构造后量子公钥加密，声称提高对抗结构性攻击的安全性并实现可扩展、线性时间解密。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在后量子时代寻找同时具备高安全边界、可扩展性和高效解码的公钥密码方案，克服经典基于代数结构的编码密码（如McEliece）易受结构攻击的弱点。

Method: 构造随机样式的生成矩阵以掩盖代数结构；使用高记忆卷积码与有向图解码器的并行数组；在解码过程中通过多项式除法有意引入强噪声（‘polynomial ambiguity’）来混淆攻击者；保持合法接收方的多项式时间解码并保证线性时间和每比特均匀开销。

Result: 作者宣称该方案提供远超Classic McEliece的安全裕度（>2^(200)），支持任意明文长度、线性时间解密和并行实现，适合长消息和硬件/软件部署。

Conclusion: 该论文提出了一种基于有向图解码并在解码阶段注入强噪声的高记忆卷积码构造，用于后量子公钥加密，声称能隐藏代数结构并抵抗已知结构性攻击，合法解密为多项式时间而攻击者需指数时间，从而获得比Classic McEliece高出约2^(200)的安全边界。

Abstract: We present a novel approach to post-quantum cryptography that employs directed-graph decryption of noise-enhanced high-memory convolutional codes. The proposed construction generates random-like generator matrices that effectively conceal algebraic structure and resist known structural attacks. Security is further reinforced by the deliberate injection of strong noise during decryption, arising from polynomial division: while legitimate recipients retain polynomial-time decoding, adversaries face exponential-time complexity. As a result, the scheme achieves cryptanalytic security margins surpassing those of Classic McEliece by factors exceeding 2^(200). Beyond its enhanced security, the method offers greater design flexibility, supporting arbitrary plaintext lengths with linear-time decryption and uniform per-bit computational cost, enabling seamless scalability to long messages. Practical deployment is facilitated by parallel arrays of directed-graph decoders, which identify the correct plaintext through polynomial ambiguity while allowing efficient hardware and software implementations. Altogether, the scheme represents a compelling candidate for robust, scalable, and quantum-resistant public-key cryptography.

### [23] [Belobog: Move Language Fuzzing Framework For Real-World Smart Contracts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02918)
*Wanxu Xia,Ziqiao Kong,Zhengwei Li,Yi Lu,Pan Li,Liqun Yang,Yang Liu,Xiapu Luo,Shaohua Li*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: Belobog, the first type-aware fuzzer for Move, builds type graphs and uses concolic execution to generate well-typed transactions, finding many real vulnerabilities and reproducing major exploits.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing fuzzers fail on Move due to its strong type system; need a type-aware fuzzer to generate well-typed transactions and discover vulnerabilities beyond type system.

Method: Constructs a type graph from Move types, generates/mutates transactions via graph traces, and uses a concolic executor to handle complex checks.

Result: On 109 real-world projects, detected 100% of critical and 79% of major audited vulnerabilities; reproduced full exploits for Cetus and Nemo without prior knowledge.

Conclusion: Belobog is effective in fuzzing Move smart contracts by ensuring type-correct transactions and combining concolic execution, achieving high vulnerability detection and reproducing known exploits.

Abstract: Move is a research-oriented programming language design for secure and verifiable smart contract development and has been widely used in managing billions of digital assets in blockchains, such as Sui and Aptos. Move features a strong static type system and explicit resource semantics to enforce safety properties such as the prevention of data races, invalid asset transfers, and entry vulnerabilities. However, smart contracts written in Move may still contain certain vulnerabilities that are beyond the reach of its type system. It is thus essential to validate Move smart contracts. Unfortunately, due to its strong type system, existing smart contract fuzzers are ineffective in producing syntactically or semantically valid transactions to test Move smart contracts. This paper introduces the first fuzzing framework, Belobog, for Move smart contracts. Belobog is type-aware and ensures that all generated and mutated transactions are well-typed. More specifically, for a target Move smart contract, Belobog first constructs a type graph based on Move's type system, and then generates or mutates a transaction based on the graph trace derived from the type graph. In order to overcome the complex checks in Move smart contracts, we further design and implement a concolic executor in Belobog. We evaluated Belobog on 109 real-world Move smart contract projects. The experimental results show that Belobog is able to detect 100\% critical and 79\% major vulnerabilities manually audited by human experts. We further selected two recent notorious incidents in Move smart contracts, i.e., Cetus and Nemo. Belobog successfully reproduced full exploits for both of them, without any prior knowledge.

</details>

*Yi Liu,Chen Qian*

Main category: cs.DC

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在GPU集群上设计流水线机制，将向量搜索任务拆分为并行计算与数据传输阶段，利用GPUDirect Async直接在GPU间或与网络之间进行异步数据传输，以实现通信与计算的重叠；可能结合分片索引、预取策略与调度以保持GPU高利用率。

Result: Fantasy在大图和大查询批量场景下显著提高搜索吞吐率，降低GPU因数据加载而造成的停滞，表现出比将数据保存在CPU/SSD并同步加载的方法更高的效率和可扩展性。

Conclusion: Fantasy通过在GPU集群中使用GPUDirect Async实现计算与数据传输流水线化，重叠查询计算与网络通信，从而提升大规模图索引的搜索吞吐率，支持更大的查询批量并减少因数据加载导致的GPU停滞。

Abstract: Vector similarity search has become a critical component in AI-driven applications such as large language models (LLMs). To achieve high recall and low latency, GPUs are utilized to exploit massive parallelism for faster query processing. However, as the number of vectors continues to grow, the graph size quickly exceeds the memory capacity of a single GPU, making it infeasible to store and process the entire index on a single GPU. Recent work uses CPU-GPU architectures to keep vectors in CPU memory or SSDs, but the loading step stalls GPU computation. We present Fantasy, an efficient system that pipelines vector search and data transfer in a GPU cluster with GPUDirect Async. Fantasy overlaps computation and network communication to significantly improve search throughput for large graphs and deliver large query batch sizes.

### [25] [DOLMA: A Data Object Level Memory Disaggregation Framework for HPC Applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02300)
*Haoyu Zheng,Shouwei Gao,Jie Ren,Wenqian Dong*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: DOLMA通过对象级内存卸载与基于访问可预测性的双缓冲远端预取，平衡本地与远端内存使用，在减少本地内存需求的同时将性能损失控制在<16%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 内存解耦有助于扩展HPC系统的内存容量与提升利用率，但远程内存访问带来的性能开销，尤其对对数据局部性敏感的计算密集型HPC应用，是主要障碍。需要一种既能节省本地内存又能将性能损失降至最低的方案。

Method: 提出基于数据对象级别的内存分离框架：智能识别并卸载适合放入远程内存的数据对象，提供定量分析以决定合适的本地内存容量，并利用双缓冲设计基于可预测访问模式进行远端预取，同时在调度上保持多线程并发以减少延迟影响。

Result: 在八个HPC工作负载和计算内核上的评估显示：平均可将本地内存使用量减少最多63%，且将性能下降限制在16%以内。

Conclusion: DOLMA能在保持多线程并发的同时，通过基于数据对象的远程内存卸载与双缓冲预取，将HPC应用的本地内存需求显著降低，并将性能下降控制在可接受范围内。

Abstract: Memory disaggregation is promising to scale memory capacity and improves utilization in HPC systems. However, the performance overhead of accessing remote memory poses a significant challenge, particularly for compute-intensive HPC applications where execution times are highly sensitive to data locality. In this work, we present DOLMA, a Data Object Level M emory dis Aggregation framework designed for HPC applications. DOLMA intelligently identifies and offloads data objects to remote memory, while providing quantitative analysis to decide a suitable local memory size. Furthermore, DOLMA leverages the predictable memory access patterns typical in HPC applications and enables remote memory prefetch via a dual-buffer design. By carefully balancing local and remote memory usage and maintaining multi-thread concurrency, DOLMA provides a flexible and efficient solution for leveraging disaggregated memory in HPC domains while minimally compromising application performance. Evaluating with eight HPC workloads and computational kernels, DOLMA limits performance degradation to less than 16% while reducing local memory usage by up to 63%, on average.

</details>

### [27] [Offloading Artificial Intelligence Workloads across the Computing Continuum by means of Active Storage Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02646)
*Alex Barceló,Sebastián A. Cajas Ordoñez,Jaydeep Samanta,Andrés L. Suárez-Cetrulo,Romila Ghosh,Ricardo Simón Carbajo,Anna Queralt*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: Design and implement a software architecture that embeds computation into storage using dataClay and mainstream Python libraries, enabling seamless distribution of AI workloads across heterogeneous devices in the computing continuum.

Result: Experimental evaluation shows improved memory consumption, reduced training times, and maintained accuracy when offloading workloads to active storage, with trade-offs in storage requirements and execution efficiency across devices.

Conclusion: Active storage in the computing continuum can significantly improve memory efficiency and training speeds for AI workloads, while maintaining model accuracy, and lowering the entry barrier for developers.

Abstract: The increasing demand for artificial intelligence (AI) workloads across diverse computing environments has driven the need for more efficient data management strategies. Traditional cloud-based architectures struggle to handle the sheer volume and velocity of AI-driven data, leading to inefficiencies in storage, computation, and data movement. This paper explores the integration of active storage systems within the computing continuum to optimize AI workload distribution.
  By embedding computation directly into storage architectures, active storage is able to reduce data transfer overhead, enhancing performance and improving resource utilization. Other existing frameworks and architectures offer mechanisms to distribute certain AI processes across distributed environments; however, they lack the flexibility and adaptability that the continuum requires, both regarding the heterogeneity of devices and the rapid-changing algorithms and models being used by domain experts and researchers.
  This article proposes a software architecture aimed at seamlessly distributing AI workloads across the computing continuum, and presents its implementation using mainstream Python libraries and dataClay, an active storage platform. The evaluation shows the benefits and trade-offs regarding memory consumption, storage requirements, training times, and execution efficiency across different devices. Experimental results demonstrate that the process of offloading workloads through active storage significantly improves memory efficiency and training speeds while maintaining accuracy. Our findings highlight the potential of active storage to revolutionize AI workload management, making distributed AI deployments more scalable and resource-efficient with a very low entry barrier for domain experts and application developers.

### [28] [Distributed and Autonomic Minimum Spanning Trees](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02683)
*Luiz A. Rodrigues,Elias P. Duarte,Luciana Arantes*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 使用VCube构建自愈生成树，保证节点入度与深度≤log_2 n，支持可扩展的最佳努力与可靠广播，并在节点故障/恢复时透明重建，仿真验证优于若干替代方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 一对多通信（one-to-all）在发送方压力大，缺乏可扩展性；需要一种能在节点频繁故障和恢复下仍保持可扩展广播能力的分布式生成树机制。

Method: 基于VCube虚拟拓扑作为底层结构和故障检测器，算法自发从任一源构造生成树，确保树中每个节点的入度和深度不超过⌈log_2 n⌉（文中表述为不超过log_2 n），并在全部进程正常时每节点度为log_2 n。提出两种基于该树的广播算法：最佳努力广播和可靠广播。

Result: 算法能从任意源建立生成树，容忍最多n-1个故障进程仍保持正确进程连通；仿真结果展示了该方法与其他方案相比在负载、延迟或恢复能力上的优势（文内有具体比较）。

Conclusion: 该文提出了一种自管理算法，用于分布式系统中构建和维护可扩展的生成树，支持广播且在节点故障/恢复时透明重建。

Abstract: The most common strategy for enabling a process in a distributed system to broadcast a message is one-to-all communication. However, this approach is not scalable, as it places a heavy load on the sender. This work presents an autonomic algorithm that enables the $n$ processes in a distributed system to build and maintain a spanning tree connecting themselves. In this context, processes are the vertices of the spanning tree. By definition, a spanning tree connects all processes without forming cycles. The proposed algorithm ensures that every vertex in the spanning tree has both an in-degree and the tree depth of at most $log_2 n$. When all processes are correct, the degree of each process is exactly $log_2 n$. A spanning tree is dynamically created from any source process and is transparently reconstructed as processes fail or recover. Up to $n-1$ processes can fail, and the correct processes remain connected through a scalable, functioning spanning tree. To build and maintain the tree, processes use the VCube virtual topology, which also serves as a failure detector. Two broadcast algorithms based on the autonomic spanning tree algorithm are presented: one for best-effort broadcast and one for reliable broadcast. Simulation results are provided, including comparisons with other alternatives.

</details>


### [29] [Designing FAIR Workflows at OLCF: Building Scalable and Reusable Ecosystems for HPC Science](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02818)
*Sean R. Wilkinson,Patrick Widener,Sarp Oral,Rafael Ferreira da Silva*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 为减少在HPC中重复开发并促进跨学科复用，本文提出基于EOSC架构、以工作流组件为单位的FAIR化模型，建议HPC中心在基础设施层面支持组件注册、元数据与发现服务。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: HPC中心的硬件、软件和安全环境与用户本地系统差异大，导致用户为特定中心定制数字制品并造成重复开发；FAIR原则提供解决共享和复用问题的框架，但现有实践大多以学科为中心形成孤岛。作者希望通过HPC中心介入打破学科壁垒。

Method: 基于EOSC-Life FAIR Workflows Collaboratory的架构，提出适用于HPC环境的模型，强调在基础设施层面设计支持富元数据与社区标准的机制，以便使单个工作流组件可被注册、描述、发现与复用。

Result: 提出组件化的FAIR模型：聚焦工作流组件的元数据标准、注册与发现机制，以及与HPC特有的部署与安全需求的对接，旨在增强跨学科复用性并延长数字制品的使用寿命。

Conclusion: 该论文主张高性能计算（HPC）中心应主动推动符合FAIR原则的生态系统，通过使工作流组件（而非整个工作流）可发现、可共享、可复用，促进跨学科协作并减少重复劳动。

Abstract: High Performance Computing (HPC) centers provide advanced infrastructure that enables scientific research at extreme scale. These centers operate with hardware configurations, software environments, and security requirements that differ substantially from most users' local systems. As a result, users often develop customized digital artifacts that are tightly coupled to a given HPC center. This practice can lead to significant duplication of effort as multiple users independently create similar solutions to common problems. The FAIR Principles offer a framework to address these challenges. Initially designed to improve data stewardship, the FAIR approach has since been extended to encompass software, workflows, models, and infrastructure. By encouraging the use of rich metadata and community standards, FAIR practices aim to make digital artifacts easier to share and reuse, both within and across scientific domains. Many FAIR initiatives have emerged within individual research communities, often aligned by discipline (e.g. bioinformatics, earth sciences). These communities have made progress in adopting FAIR practices, but their domain-specific nature can lead to silos that limit broader collaboration. Thus, we propose that HPC centers play a more active role in fostering FAIR ecosystems that support research across multiple disciplines. This requires designing infrastructure that enables researchers to discover, share, and reuse computational components more effectively. Here, we build on the architecture of the European Open Science Cloud (EOSC) EOSC-Life FAIR Workflows Collaboratory to propose a model tailored to the needs of HPC. Rather than focusing on entire workflows, we emphasize the importance of making individual workflow components FAIR. This component-based approach better supports the diverse and evolving needs of HPC users while maximizing the long-term value of their work.

</details>

### [30] [An Improved Ensemble-Based Machine Learning Model with Feature Optimization for Early Diabetes Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02023)
*Md. Najmul Islam,Md. Miner Hossain Rimon,Shah Sadek-E-Akbor Shamim,Zarif Mohaimen Fahad,Md. Jehadul Islam Mony,Md. Jalal Uddin Chowdhury*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 利用BRFSS大规模健康数据，结合SMOTE/Tomek处理不平衡、多模型与堆叠集成，研究实现了高ROC-AUC（≈0.99）和高准确率（94.82%）的糖尿病早期预测，并提供了移动应用实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 由于糖尿病早期检测困难且临床决策需可解释的模型，研究旨在利用大型健康调查数据构建既准确又可解释的分类框架，便于临床应用与患者自我监测。

Method: 采用2015年BRFSS数据（约253,680条记录，22个数值特征），通过SMOTE和Tomek Links处理类别不平衡，训练多种监督学习模型并尝试堆叠集成（XGBoost与KNN作为元学习器），评估指标包括准确率、ROC-AUC和PR-AUC。

Result: 单模型（Random Forest、XGBoost、CatBoost、LightGBM）取得约0.96的ROC-AUC；堆叠集成（XGBoost+KNN）达到94.82%准确率、ROC-AUC 0.989、PR-AUC 0.991，表现最佳；并实现了移动端应用原型。

Conclusion: 该研究成功利用BRFSS数据并通过机器学习模型（包括随机森林、XGBoost、CatBoost、LightGBM及堆叠集成）实现了高精度的糖尿病预测，并开发了React Native+Flask的移动应用以支持早期监测。

Abstract: Diabetes is a serious worldwide health issue, and successful intervention depends on early detection. However, overlapping risk factors and data asymmetry make prediction difficult. To use extensive health survey data to create a machine learning framework for diabetes classification that is both accurate and comprehensible, to produce results that will aid in clinical decision-making. Using the BRFSS dataset, we assessed a number of supervised learning techniques. SMOTE and Tomek Links were used to correct class imbalance. To improve prediction performance, both individual models and ensemble techniques such as stacking were investigated. The 2015 BRFSS dataset, which includes roughly 253,680 records with 22 numerical features, is used in this study. Strong ROC-AUC performance of approximately 0.96 was attained by the individual models Random Forest, XGBoost, CatBoost, and LightGBM.The stacking ensemble with XGBoost and KNN yielded the best overall results with 94.82\% accuracy, ROC-AUC of 0.989, and PR-AUC of 0.991, indicating a favourable balance between recall and precision. In our study, we proposed and developed a React Native-based application with a Python Flask backend to support early diabetes prediction, providing users with an accessible and efficient health monitoring tool.

</details>


### [31] [Pharmacophore-based design by learning on voxel grids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02031)
*Omar Mahmood,Pedro O. Pinheiro,Richard Bonneau,Saeed Saremi,Vishnu Sresht*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出基于体素的药效团到 SMILES 的生成方法 VoxCap，支持高质量去新分子生成与极快的生成+2D筛选快速搜索，兼顾多样性与可扩展性，显著优于传统暴力筛选。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统基于药效团-形状的虚拟筛选虽然在命中多样化和骨架跳跃方面有效，但对大规模分子库不具可扩展性，且受限于现有库化合物；因此需要一种既能保留药效团-形状比对优势又能高效生成新候选、扩展化学空间的方法。

Method: 引入 VoxCap —— 一种 voxel captioning 模型，将分子体素化的药效团-形状表示作为输入，生成对应的 SMILES。提出两种应用流程：1) 去新设计（de-novo），直接生成与查询分子药效团-形状相似且结构多样的新分子；2) 快速搜索，将生成器与廉价的2D子结构相似性检索结合，先生成候选再用2D滤过以快速鉴别命中。模型利用体素化生成与评分替代对每个库分子构建并比对3D构象的暴力搜索。

Result: VoxCap 在去新设计任务中比现有方法显著生成出更多多样化的命中分子；在快速搜索流程中，将计算时间降低了数量级（orders of magnitude），并能为所有查询返回命中，支持对大型库的可行搜索。

Conclusion: VoxCap 提出了一种基于体素（voxel）表征的药效团（pharmacophore）生成模型，能从体素化分子表示生成 SMILES，从而在去新设计和快速搜索任务中同时提升多样性与效率。该方法在生成多样化去新命中体上的表现显著优于此前方法，并在与快速搜索流程结合时将计算时间降低数个数量级，能够为所有查询分子返回命中，使得对原本不可行的大型库搜索成为可能。

Abstract: Ligand-based drug discovery (LBDD) relies on making use of known binders to a protein target to find structurally diverse molecules similarly likely to bind. This process typically involves a brute force search of the known binder (query) against a molecular library using some metric of molecular similarity. One popular approach overlays the pharmacophore-shape profile of the known binder to 3D conformations enumerated for each of the library molecules, computes overlaps, and picks a set of diverse library molecules with high overlaps. While this virtual screening workflow has had considerable success in hit diversification, scaffold hopping, and patent busting, it scales poorly with library sizes and restricts candidate generation to existing library compounds. Leveraging recent advances in voxel-based generative modelling, we propose a pharmacophore-based generative model and workflows that address the scaling and fecundity issues of conventional pharmacophore-based virtual screening. We introduce \emph{VoxCap}, a voxel captioning method for generating SMILES strings from voxelised molecular representations. We propose two workflows as practical use cases as well as benchmarks for pharmacophore-based generation: \emph{de-novo} design, in which we aim to generate new molecules with high pharmacophore-shape similarities to query molecules, and fast search, which aims to combine generative design with a cheap 2D substructure similarity search for efficient hit identification. Our results show that VoxCap significantly outperforms previous methods in generating diverse \textit{de-novo} hits. When combined with our fast search workflow, VoxCap reduces computational time by orders of magnitude while returning hits for all query molecules, enabling the search of large libraries that are intractable to search by brute force.

</details>


### [32] [PIBNet: a Physics-Inspired Boundary Network for Multiple Scattering Simulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02049)
*Rémi Marsal,Stéphanie Chaillat*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出PIBNet：用物理启发的多尺度图神经网络近似BEM的边界解迹，加速多重散射模拟，同时在准确性和泛化性上优于现有学习方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: BEM能有效处理无界均匀域中的多重散射，但求解边界积分方程得到边界解迹是主要计算瓶颈。基于学习的近似有望加速这一过程并保持足够精度。

Method: 方法包括：将障碍物及其远程相互作用用图结构建模；引入新颖的多尺度图神经网络架构来模拟多重散射；训练基于多个合成数据集的基准并评估泛化性能。

Result: 在多个数据集上，PIBNet优于现有学习方法，并对障碍物数量增加表现出更好的泛化能力。作者提供了代码仓库。

Conclusion: 该论文提出了PIBNet，一种基于物理启发的图神经网络，用于近似边界元方法（BEM）中求解多重散射问题的边界解迹，从而显著降低首要计算瓶颈。

Abstract: The boundary element method (BEM) provides an efficient numerical framework for solving multiple scattering problems in unbounded homogeneous domains, since it reduces the discretization to the domain boundaries, thereby condensing the computational complexity. The procedure first consists in determining the solution trace on the boundaries of the domain by solving a boundary integral equation, after which the volumetric solution can be recovered at low computational cost with a boundary integral representation. As the first step of the BEM represents the main computational bottleneck, we introduce PIBNet, a learning-based approach designed to approximate the solution trace. The method leverages a physics-inspired graph-based strategy to model obstacles and their long-range interactions efficiently. Then, we introduce a novel multiscale graph neural network architecture for simulating the multiple scattering. To train and evaluate our network, we present a benchmark consisting of several datasets of different types of multiple scattering problems. The results indicate that our approach not only surpasses existing state-of-the-art learning-based methods on the considered tasks but also exhibits superior generalization to settings with an increased number of obstacles. github.com/ENSTA-U2IS-AI/pibnet

</details>


### [33] [Contextual Gating within the Transformer Stack: Synergistic Feature Modulation for Enhanced Lyrical Classification and Calibration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02053)
*M. A. Gameiro*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 在BERT编码器中用Contextual Gating中层注入低维结构特征，比输出层融合更能提升歌词二分类性能与概率校准，SFL Transformer达到了新的最优结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 动机是探索如何更有效地将辅助结构性信息（例如歌词的结构特征）与强大的上下文化语义表示（来自预训练Transformer）融合，以提升分类性能并获得更可靠的概率输出。作者假设在Transformer中间层注入辅助信息优于最终层融合。

Method: 提出SFL Transformer：在预训练BERT编码器的隐藏状态序列上使用Contextual Gating（Intermediate SFL）将低维结构特征Fstruct调制到深层语义特征Hseq中，而非在输出层进行特征级联或简单融合。训练并在UMAP降维的歌词嵌入构造的二分类任务上评估模型，报告准确率、Macro F1、ECE和Log Loss。

Result: SFL Transformer在所设二分类任务上取得Accuracy=0.9910、Macro F1=0.9910，优于此前SFL模型（Accuracy=0.9894）；且模型校准良好，ECE=0.0081，Log Loss=0.0489。

Conclusion: 论文结论是：在Transformer编码器堆栈中间注入结构性辅助特征（通过Contextual Gating的中间SFL机制）能比在输出层融合更有效地结合语义与结构信息，从而在歌词内容二分类任务上显著提升性能并保持良好校准。

Abstract: This study introduces a significant architectural advancement in feature fusion for lyrical content classification by integrating auxiliary structural features directly into the self-attention mechanism of a pre-trained Transformer. I propose the SFL Transformer, a novel deep learning model that utilizes a Contextual Gating mechanism (an Intermediate SFL) to modulate the sequence of hidden states within the BERT encoder stack, rather than fusing features at the final output layer. This approach modulates the deep, contextualized semantic features (Hseq) using low-dimensional structural cues (Fstruct). The model is applied to a challenging binary classification task derived from UMAP-reduced lyrical embeddings. The SFL Transformer achieved an Accuracy of 0.9910 and a Macro F1 score of 0.9910, significantly improving the state-of-the-art established by the previously published SFL model (Accuracy 0.9894). Crucially, this Contextual Gating strategy maintained exceptional reliability, with a low Expected Calibration Error (ECE = 0.0081) and Log Loss (0.0489). This work validates the hypothesis that injecting auxiliary context mid-stack is the most effective means of synergistically combining structural and semantic information, creating a model with both superior discriminative power and high-fidelity probability estimates.

</details>


### [34] [Opening the Black Box: An Explainable, Few-shot AI4E Framework Informed by Physics and Expert Knowledge for Materials Engineering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02057)
*Haoxiang Zhang,Ruihao Yuan,Lihui Zhang,Yushi Luo,Qiang Zhang,Pan Ding,Xiaodong Ren,Weijie Xing,Niu Gao,Jishan Chen,Chubo Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 基于32样本的物理引导少样本框架，通过物理约束合成数据和符号回归+差分进化的嵌套优化发现可解释本构方程，88%准确率并具机理可解释性，可用于过程优化与虚拟数据生成，促进高风险工业领域AI可信应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 工业AI4E推广受限于高质量数据稀缺与黑箱模型不可解释性，尤其在航空等安全敏感领域，需在少样本下构建既可信又有物理解释能力的模型。

Method: 从32个实验样本出发，进行三阶段物理可行合成数据增强（差分噪声注入、物理约束强制、参数间关系保持）；采用嵌套优化的本构方程发现——符号回归搜索方程结构、差分进化优化参数，再用混合全局-局部优化精细拟合；最终用所得可解释方程进行预测与生成数据以提升其他模型表现。

Result: 发现的本构方程在热裂倾向预测上达88%准确率，并提供了热、几何、冶金耦合机理的定量解释；该方程还能用于工艺优化和高保真虚拟数据生成，从而提升下游数据驱动模型的准确性。

Conclusion: 该论文通过将物理与专家知识系统性地融入模型，实现了在极少样本条件下可解释的AI4E框架，成功预测并解释了修复焊接中的热裂倾向，验证了可用于过程优化和高保真虚拟数据生成的多功能性。

Abstract: The industrial adoption of Artificial Intelligence for Engineering (AI4E) faces two fundamental bottlenecks: scarce high-quality data and the lack of interpretability in black-box models-particularly critical in safety-sensitive sectors like aerospace. We present an explainable, few-shot AI4E framework that is systematically informed by physics and expert knowledge throughout its architecture. Starting from only 32 experimental samples in an aerial K439B superalloy castings repair welding case, we first augment physically plausible synthetic data through a three-stage protocol: differentiated noise injection calibrated to process variabilities, enforcement of hard physical constraints, and preservation of inter-parameter relationships. We then employ a nested optimization strategy for constitutive model discovery, where symbolic regression explores equation structures while differential evolution optimizes parameters, followed by intensive parameter refinement using hybrid global-local optimization. The resulting interpretable constitutive equation achieves 88% accuracy in predicting hot-cracking tendency. This equation not only provides quantitative predictions but also delivers explicit physical insight, revealing how thermal, geometric, and metallurgical mechanisms couple to drive cracking-thereby advancing engineers' cognitive understanding of the process. Furthermore, the constitutive equation serves as a multi-functional tool for process optimization and high-fidelity virtual data generation, enabling accuracy improvements in other data-driven models. Our approach provides a general blueprint for developing trustworthy AI systems that embed engineering domain knowledge directly into their architecture, enabling reliable adoption in high-stakes industrial applications where data is limited but physical understanding is available.

</details>


### [35] [Ada-MoGE: Adaptive Mixture of Gaussian Expert Model for Time Series Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02061)
*Zhenliang Ni,Xiaowen Ma,Zhenkai Wu,Shuai Xiao,Han Shu,Xinghao Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出Ada-MoGE：基于频谱信息自适应决定专家数并用高斯带通滤波平滑频域分解，解决MoE在频率覆盖上的不平衡问题，并以小参数量实现SOTA表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多变量时间序列的主导频率会随数据的谱分布变化而漂移，固定专家数的MoE难以覆盖不断变化的频谱导致重要信息遗漏或噪声引入，需自适应调整专家数量与频带划分以匹配输入数据的频率分布。

Method: 提出Ada-MoGE：结合光谱强度与频率响应自适应决定专家数目；用高斯带通滤波对频域特征进行平滑分解，避免直接带截断引入噪声；整体为基于高斯混合专家的模块并在多变量时间序列预测任务上训练与评估。

Result: 在六个公开基准数据集上，Ada-MoGE以约0.2M参数量达到了SOTA性能，显示其在参数效率与泛化能力上的优势。

Conclusion: 本文提出的Ada-MoGE通过自适应确定专家数量并使用高斯带通滤波平滑频域分解，有效缓解了频率覆盖不平衡问题，实验显示在六个公开基准上以仅0.2M参数取得了最先进的性能，结论可信且具有实际应用价值。

Abstract: Multivariate time series forecasts are widely used, such as industrial, transportation and financial forecasts. However, the dominant frequencies in time series may shift with the evolving spectral distribution of the data. Traditional Mixture of Experts (MoE) models, which employ a fixed number of experts, struggle to adapt to these changes, resulting in frequency coverage imbalance issue. Specifically, too few experts can lead to the overlooking of critical information, while too many can introduce noise. To this end, we propose Ada-MoGE, an adaptive Gaussian Mixture of Experts model. Ada-MoGE integrates spectral intensity and frequency response to adaptively determine the number of experts, ensuring alignment with the input data's frequency distribution. This approach prevents both information loss due to an insufficient number of experts and noise contamination from an excess of experts. Additionally, to prevent noise introduction from direct band truncation, we employ Gaussian band-pass filtering to smoothly decompose the frequency domain features, further optimizing the feature representation. The experimental results show that our model achieves state-of-the-art performance on six public benchmarks with only 0.2 million parameters.

</details>


### [36] [DPWMixer: Dual-Path Wavelet Mixer for Long-Term Time Series Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02070)
*Li Qianyang,Zhang Xingjun,Wang Shaoxun,Wei Jia*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出 DPWMixer：用无损 Haar 小波金字塔替代池化，结合全局线性与补丁式 MLP-Mixer 的双路径趋势建模，并通过通道平稳性加权的自适应多尺度融合，提升 LTSF 性能且计算高效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 Transformer 模型虽善于捕获长程依赖，但面临二次复杂度与在数据稀疏下的过拟合；线性高效模型难以刻画复杂的局部非线性；而传统多尺度框架使用平均池化导致频谱混叠及高频瞬态的不可逆丢失。为此作者提出用无损小波分解保持信息并更好分离趋势与细节。

Method: 方法包括：1) 用无损 Haar 小波金字塔替代平均池化，进行正交分解以分离多尺度分量；2) 设计双路径趋势混合器（Dual-Path Trend Mixer）：一条路径为全局线性映射处理宏观趋势，另一条路径为基于补丁的 MLP-Mixer 处理微观非线性动态；3) 采用自适应多尺度融合模块，根据通道的平稳性对不同尺度的预测按权重进行合成。

Result: 在八个公开基准上进行大量实验，结果显示 DPWMixer 在长期时间序列预测任务上相较于多种最新基线方法具有一致的性能提升。并已开源代码。

Conclusion: DPWMixer 提出了一种基于无损 Haar 小波金字塔的双路径架构，能够在保持信息不丢失的前提下分离趋势与局部波动，并通过全局线性映射与基于补丁的 MLP-Mixer 分别建模宏观趋势与微观动态，最终通过自适应多尺度融合按通道平稳性加权合成预测结果，展示了在八个基准数据集上优于现有方法的稳定性能提升。

Abstract: Long-term time series forecasting (LTSF) is a critical task in computational intelligence. While Transformer-based models effectively capture long-range dependencies, they often suffer from quadratic complexity and overfitting due to data sparsity. Conversely, efficient linear models struggle to depict complex non-linear local dynamics. Furthermore, existing multi-scale frameworks typically rely on average pooling, which acts as a non-ideal low-pass filter, leading to spectral aliasing and the irreversible loss of high-frequency transients. In response, this paper proposes DPWMixer, a computationally efficient Dual-Path architecture. The framework is built upon a Lossless Haar Wavelet Pyramid that replaces traditional pooling, utilizing orthogonal decomposition to explicitly disentangle trends and local fluctuations without information loss. To process these components, we design a Dual-Path Trend Mixer that integrates a global linear mapping for macro-trend anchoring and a flexible patch-based MLP-Mixer for micro-dynamic evolution. Finally, An adaptive multi-scale fusion module then integrates predictions from diverse scales, weighted by channel stationarity to optimize synthesis. Extensive experiments on eight public benchmarks demonstrate that our method achieves a consistent improvement over state-of-the-art baselines. The code is available at https://github.com/hit636/DPWMixer.

</details>


### [37] [TokenPowerBench: Benchmarking the Power Consumption of LLM Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.03024)
*Chenxu Niu,Wei Zhang,Jie Li,Yongjian Zhao,Tongyang Wang,Xi Wang,Yong Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: TokenPowerBench：首个轻量可扩展的LLM推理能耗基准，提供无专用设备的多层功耗测量与相位归因，支持多种模型与配置，已开源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前基准集中在训练或推理性能，缺乏对推理阶段能耗的测量与分析工具，而推理占LLM服务能耗绝大多数。

Method: 提供声明式配置接口、无需专用功率表的测量层（捕获GPU/节点/系统级功耗）、以及相位对齐的度量管道，将能量归因到每次请求的prefill与decode阶段；支持批量、上下文长度、并行策略、量化等变量。

Result: 在Llama、Falcon、Qwen、Mistral系列模型上从1B到Llama3-405B进行评测，展示如何通过调整配置影响每token焦耳等能效指标，并将工具开源。

Conclusion: TokenPowerBench填补了LLM推理能耗评测的空白，提供轻量可扩展的基准并开源，可帮助部署方优化能效与成本。

Abstract: Large language model (LLM) services now answer billions of queries per day, and industry reports show that inference, not training, accounts for more than 90% of total power consumption. However, existing benchmarks focus on either training/fine-tuning or performance of inference and provide little support for power consumption measurement and analysis of inference. We introduce TokenPowerBench, the first lightweight and extensible benchmark designed for LLM-inference power consumption studies. The benchmark combines (i) a declarative configuration interface covering model choice, prompt set, and inference engine, (ii) a measurement layer that captures GPU-, node-, and system-level power without specialized power meters, and (iii) a phase-aligned metrics pipeline that attributes energy to the prefill and decode stages of every request. These elements make it straight-forward to explore the power consumed by an LLM inference run; furthermore, by varying batch size, context length, parallelism strategy and quantization, users can quickly assess how each setting affects joules per token and other energy-efficiency metrics. We evaluate TokenPowerBench on four of the most widely used model series (Llama, Falcon, Qwen, and Mistral). Our experiments cover from 1 billion parameters up to the frontier-scale Llama3-405B model. Furthermore, we release TokenPowerBench as open source to help users to measure power consumption, forecast operating expenses, and meet sustainability targets when deploying LLM services.

</details>


### [38] [HTG-GCL: Leveraging Hierarchical Topological Granularity from Cellular Complexes for Graph Contrastive Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02073)
*Qirui Ji,Bin Qin,Yifan Jin,Yunze Zhao,Chuxiong Sun,Changwen Zheng,Jianwen Cao,Jiangmeng Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出HTG-GCL：用多尺度环形细胞复形构造拓扑视图，并通过多粒度解耦对比与不确定性加权筛除误导性粒度，提升GCL在多任务下的表示能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有GCL的结构增强难以自动识别下游任务所需的关键拓扑结构，且不同任务对拓扑粒度的需求不同，单一或固定粒度的视图会引入噪声或丢失关键信息。

Method: 对同一图进行变换以生成多尺度的基于环的细胞复形作为不同拓扑粒度的视图；在对比学习中采用多粒度解耦对比损失，并对每一粒度引入基于不确定性估计的权重来抑制误导性语义；在训练时联合优化表示器和粒度权重。

Result: 在多种基准数据集上（如图分类与节点分类任务）HTG-GCL显示出优越性能，表明通过层级拓扑粒度建模与不确定性加权可以获得更具判别性的图表示。

Conclusion: HTG-GCL通过引入基于环的细胞复形构建多尺度拓扑视图，并结合多粒度解耦对比与不确定性加权机制，能更好捕捉任务相关的拓扑信息，从而提升图表示学习效果。

Abstract: Graph contrastive learning (GCL) aims to learn discriminative semantic invariance by contrasting different views of the same graph that share critical topological patterns. However, existing GCL approaches with structural augmentations often struggle to identify task-relevant topological structures, let alone adapt to the varying coarse-to-fine topological granularities required across different downstream tasks. To remedy this issue, we introduce Hierarchical Topological Granularity Graph Contrastive Learning (HTG-GCL), a novel framework that leverages transformations of the same graph to generate multi-scale ring-based cellular complexes, embodying the concept of topological granularity, thereby generating diverse topological views. Recognizing that a certain granularity may contain misleading semantics, we propose a multi-granularity decoupled contrast and apply a granularity-specific weighting mechanism based on uncertainty estimation. Comprehensive experiments on various benchmarks demonstrate the effectiveness of HTG-GCL, highlighting its superior performance in capturing meaningful graph representations through hierarchical topological information.

</details>

Result: 仿真与真实数据实验表明，该方法在下游回归任务上相较于传统特征提取技术有明显性能提升，能更好地提取、融合并保持与任务相关的多模态信息，同时缓解非IID下的表示漂移和遗忘问题。

Abstract: This study focuses on the feature extraction problem in multi-modal data regression. The method integrates multi-modal information extraction and contrastive learning mechanisms, and can adapt to different neural network structures as the latent mapping functions for data of each modality. It supports each client to independently learn low-dimensional representations of multi-modal data, and can flexibly control the degree of retention of effective information about the response variable in the predictive variables within the low-dimensional features through parameter tuning. The multi-constraint learning framework constructed by the method guarantees regression accuracy using Mean Squared Error loss. Through the synergistic effect of mutual information preservation constraint, symmetric Kullback-Leibler divergence constraint, and inter-model contrastive constraint, it achieves the retention of task-related information, the extraction, fusion, and alignment of multi-modal features, and the mitigation of representation drift and catastrophic forgetting in non-IID scenarios, respectively. This ensures that the feature extraction process always centers on improving the performance of downstream regression tasks. Experimental results from simulations and real-world data analysis demonstrate that the proposed method achieves more significant performance improvement on downstream regression tasks compared with classical feature extraction techniques.

Abstract: Graph classification has gained significant attention due to its applications in chemistry, social networks, and bioinformatics. While Graph Neural Networks (GNNs) effectively capture local structural patterns, they often overlook global topological features that are critical for robust representation learning. In this work, we propose GraphTCL, a dual-view contrastive learning framework that integrates structural embeddings from GNNs with topological embeddings derived from persistent homology. By aligning these complementary views through a cross-view contrastive loss, our method enhances representation quality and improves classification performance. Extensive experiments on benchmark datasets, including TU and OGB molecular graphs, demonstrate that GraphTCL consistently outperforms state-of-the-art baselines. This study highlights the importance of topology-aware contrastive learning for advancing graph representation methods.

### [41] [How Market Volatility Shapes Algorithmic Collusion: A Comparative Analysis of Learning-Based Pricing Algorithms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02134)
*Aheer Sravon,Md. Ibrahim,Devdyuti Mazumder,Ridwan Al Aziz*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 研究表明市场结构和需求不确定性决定算法化定价的反竞争风险；DDPG最易促成合谋，Logit对冲击最脆弱，Hotelling最稳健，Linear在冲击下利润反而上升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实中自主定价算法日益普及，但在更接近真实市场的随机需求条件下，这些算法如何影响竞争格局尚缺系统性研究。研究旨在填补算法、市场结构与需求不确定性三者交互对竞争结果影响的空白。

Method: 选取Q-Learning、PSO、Double DQN、DDPG四种定价算法，在Logit、Hotelling、Linear三种二重垄断模型中进行大量仿真实验。需求冲击通过自回归过程生成多种随机情形。采用利润和价格为基础的合谋指数来量化反竞争行为，比较算法在不同市场结构和冲击强度下的表现。

Result: 在稳定需求下，多数强化学习算法能维持高于竞争均衡的价格，DDPG最易导致合谋结果。加入需求冲击后：Logit市场绩效大幅下降，Hotelling市场稳健性高，Linear市场出现冲击诱发的利润上升。算法相对排序在各种环境中一致。

Conclusion: 在不同市场结构和需求不确定性下，强化学习算法表现出显著的倾向于维持超竞争价格，尤其是DDPG。市场结构决定性地影响算法表现：Logit市场对需求冲击高度敏感、Hotelling市场相对稳健、Linear市场在冲击下反而利润上升。尽管绝对绩效随环境变化显著，算法间的相对排名保持一致。

Abstract: Autonomous pricing algorithms are increasingly influencing competition in digital markets; however, their behavior under realistic demand conditions remains largely unexamined. This paper offers a thorough analysis of four pricing algorithms -- Q-Learning, PSO, Double DQN, and DDPG -- across three classic duopoly models (Logit, Hotelling, Linear) and under various demand-shock regimes created by auto-regressive processes. By utilizing profit- and price-based collusion indices, we investigate how the interactions among algorithms, market structure, and stochastic demand collaboratively influence competitive outcomes. Our findings reveal that reinforcement-learning algorithms often sustain supra-competitive prices under stable demand, with DDPG demonstrating the most pronounced collusive tendencies. Demand shocks produce notably varied effects: Logit markets suffer significant performance declines, Hotelling markets remain stable, and Linear markets experience shock-induced profit inflation. Despite marked changes in absolute performance, the relative rankings of the algorithms are consistent across different environments. These results underscore the critical importance of market structure and demand uncertainty in shaping algorithmic competition, while also contributing to the evolving policy discussions surrounding autonomous pricing behavior.

### [42] [CLEF: Clinically-Guided Contrastive Learning for Electrocardiogram Foundation Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02180)
*Yuxuan Shu,Peter H. Charlton,Fahim Kawsar,Jussi Hernesniemi,Mohammad Malekzadeh*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 用临床风险评分加权负样本的对比学习（CLEF），在大规模无标签12导联ECG上自监督预训练，能显著提升单导联下游分类与回归表现，且实现可扩展的远程监测应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自监督ECG预训练方法未充分利用可获得的临床元数据，作者希望引入领域知识（临床风险评分）以改进表征学习，使无标签大数据的预训练更符合临床差异性，提升单导联可穿戴设备心电诊断性能。

Method: 提出“clinically-guided contrastive learning”，用已有临床风险评分自适应加权负样本对，令ECG嵌入的相似性与患者间临床差异对齐，并设计处理缺失元数据的机制。在MIMIC-IV 12导联（161K患者）上训练三种规模的单导联基础模型（CLEF）；与多种基线和自监督方法比较，在7个外部数据集共18个任务上评估。

Conclusion: 该论文提出了一种利用临床风险评分对比学习的自监督预训练方法（CLEF），在单导联ECG任务上显著提升了下游分类和回归性能，尤其在仅用常规临床元数据且无需每例标签情况下表现优秀。

Abstract: The electrocardiogram (ECG) is a key diagnostic tool in cardiovascular health. Single-lead ECG recording is integrated into both clinical-grade and consumer wearables. While self-supervised pretraining of foundation models on unlabeled ECGs improves diagnostic performance, existing approaches do not incorporate domain knowledge from clinical metadata. We introduce a novel contrastive learning approach that utilizes an established clinical risk score to adaptively weight negative pairs: clinically-guided contrastive learning. It aligns the similarities of ECG embeddings with clinically meaningful differences between subjects, with an explicit mechanism to handle missing metadata. On 12-lead ECGs from 161K patients in the MIMIC-IV dataset, we pretrain single-lead ECG foundation models at three scales, collectively called CLEF, using only routinely collected metadata without requiring per-sample ECG annotations. We evaluate CLEF on 18 clinical classification and regression tasks across 7 held-out datasets, and benchmark against 5 foundation model baselines and 3 self-supervised algorithms. When pretrained on 12-lead ECG data and tested on lead-I data, CLEF outperforms self-supervised foundation model baselines: the medium-sized CLEF achieves average AUROC improvements of at least 2.6% in classification and average reductions in MAEs of at least 3.2% in regression. Comparing with existing self-supervised learning algorithms, CLEF improves the average AUROC by at least 1.8%. Moreover, when pretrained only on lead-I data for classification tasks, CLEF performs comparably to the state-of-the-art ECGFounder, which was trained in a supervised manner. Overall, CLEF enables more accurate and scalable single-lead ECG analysis, advancing remote health monitoring. Code and pretrained CLEF models are available at: github.com/Nokia-Bell-Labs/ecg-foundation-model.

### [43] [Enforcing Orderedness to Improve Feature Consistency](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02194)
*Sophie L. Wang,Alex Quach,Nithin Parsan,John J. Yang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: OSAE enforces ordered, deterministic sparse representations, theoretically fixing permutation ambiguity and empirically increasing feature consistency versus prior nested SAE methods.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: SAE features vary across seeds and hyperparameters; need for consistent, interpretable features with unique identification.

Method: Introduce Ordered Sparse Autoencoders extending Matryoshka SAEs by enforcing strict ordering of latent dimensions and deterministically using every feature dimension without sampling approximations.

Result: Theoretical proof that OSAEs resolve permutation non-identifiability in identifiable sparse dictionary learning; empirical improvement in consistency on Gemma2-2B and Pythia-70M compared to Matryoshka baselines.

Conclusion: OSAEs provide ordered, deterministic latent features that reduce permutation non-identifiability and improve feature consistency.

Abstract: Sparse autoencoders (SAEs) have been widely used for interpretability of neural networks, but their learned features often vary across seeds and hyperparameter settings. We introduce Ordered Sparse Autoencoders (OSAE), which extend Matryoshka SAEs by (1) establishing a strict ordering of latent features and (2) deterministically using every feature dimension, avoiding the sampling-based approximations of prior nested SAE methods. Theoretically, we show that OSAEs resolve permutation non-identifiability in settings of sparse dictionary learning where solutions are unique (up to natural symmetries). Empirically on Gemma2-2B and Pythia-70M, we show that OSAEs can help improve consistency compared to Matryoshka baselines.
